# All 50 Coordination Exercise Cards

**Focus:** Coordination under duress, balance-integrated object control, visual scanning, football catch transfer, and multi-limb timing.

**Source note:** Authoring format follows `exercise_card_details_for_llm.md`. `Purpose.txt` was searched for but not located in the accessible File Library results.
